V_R52_PERFORMING_ACCOUNTS		varchar2(100 BYTE):='';
V_R52_NON_PERMORMIINGA_ACCOUNTS		varchar2(100 BYTE):='';

BEGIN 

delete from BRF40A_SUMMARYTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
delete from BRF40B_SUMMARYTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;

select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_OUTSTANDING_BALANCE from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_PROFIT_SUSPENSE from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102B';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_SPECIFIE_PROVISION from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102C';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_OTHER_ALLOATE from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102D';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_NORMAL_ASSET from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND ASST_CATEGORY = 'SUB-NORMAL';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_WATCH_LIST_ASSET from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND ASST_CATEGORY = 'SUB-WATCH-LIST';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_STANDARD_ASSET from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND ASST_CATEGORY = 'SUB-STD';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_DOUBFUL_ASSET from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND ASST_CATEGORY IN ('DBF1','DBF2','DBF3');
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_LOSS_ASSET from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND ASST_CATEGORY = 'LOS';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_NORMAL_SPECIFIC from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102J';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_WATCH_LIST_SPECIFIC from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102K';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_STANDARD_SPECIFIC from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102L';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_DOUBFUL_SPECIFIC from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102M';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_LOSS_SPECIFIC from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102N';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_CURRENT from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_2 = 'Current Dues';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_LESSTHAN_30 from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_3 = 'LESS THAN 30 DAYS';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_90DAYS from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_3 = '30 - 90 days';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_120DAYS from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_3 = '90 - 120 days';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_180DAYS from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_3 = '120180 days';
select round(nvl(sum(abs(ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC))/1000,0)) into V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_OVER_180DAYS from BRF40_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE AND REPORT_LABEL_1='ROW102' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1= 'ROW102A' AND REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_3 = 'Over 180 days';
    V_R11_TOTAL_PAST:=V_R11_LESSTHAN_30+V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_90DAYS+V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_120DAYS+V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_180DAYS+V_R11_EXCLUSIVE_OVER_180DAYS ;
